[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * Lookup a String key to a String value.[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: * This class represents the simplest form of a string to string map.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: * It has a benefit over a map in that it can create the result on[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: * demand based on the key.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:     * Looks up a String key to a String value.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:     * The internal implementation may use any mechanism to return the value.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:     * The simplest implementation is to use a Map. However, virtually any[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:     * implementation is possible.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:     * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:     * Or, a numeric based implementation could be created that treats the key[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:     * as an integer, increments the value and return the result as a string -[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and the evaluation report, I have identified the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of this critical Log4Shell vulnerability:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Chain:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. User-controlled input enters log messages [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;35mlogger.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[39muserInput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mMessagePatternConverter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` detects `[0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32m"[0m[39m` pattern in the log message[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Triggers `[0m[1;35mconfig.getSubst[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which uses `StrSubstitutor`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `StrSubstitutor` extracts variable names and calls `[0m[1;35mInterpolator.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. `Interpolator` routes `[0m[32m"jndi:"[0m[39m` prefix to `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. `JndiLookup` performs `[0m[1;35mInitialContext.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with user-controlled URL[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Remote JNDI lookup to attacker-controlled LDAP/RMI server enables RCE[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Causes:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `JndiLookup` is hardcoded in `Interpolator`'s default constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m66[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` performs JNDI lookups without URL scheme validation[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The `ENABLE_JNDI` flag exists but defaults to `true` and has no system property [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrol[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `MessagePatternConverter` unconditionally processes `[0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32m"[0m[39m` patterns in log [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI need to retrieve additional code to finalize the fix strategy:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<file>core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.jav[0m[1;92ma:31[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m40[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfile[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<file>core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/pattern/MessagePatternConver[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mter.jav[0m[1;92ma:24[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m39[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfile[0m[39m>[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLet me also check if there are any existing constants or patterns for controlling [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<file>core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/helpers/Constants.jav[0m[1;92ma:20[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m58[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfile[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNow I'll formulate a comprehensive fix strategy based on defense-in-depth [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprinciples:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Disable JNDI Lookup by Default[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Modify JndiLookup to disable JNDI lookups by default**[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocation: `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Change the `ENABLE_JNDI` static field initialization from `true` to `false` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcurrently at line [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add a system property constant to control this behavior[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Initialize `ENABLE_JNDI` by reading a system property [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m using `PropertiesUtil`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The default should be `false` for security[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add the system property constant**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocation: `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/helpers/Constants.java`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add a new constant: `public static final String LOG4J_ENABLE_JNDI_LOOKUP = [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m;`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This follows the existing pattern of system properties in this file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m29[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m36[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Update JndiLookup initialization**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocation: `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Replace the simple `private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI = true;` with [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization that reads from system property[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Use [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getBooleanProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mConstants.LOG4J_ENABLE_JNDI_LOOK[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUP, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Default to `false` if the property is not set[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Secondary Fix: Add URL Scheme Validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDefense-in-Depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLocation: `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEven when JNDI is enabled, add URL scheme validation in the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m53[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Before performing the JNDI lookup, validate the JNDI name scheme[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Only allow safe schemes: `[0m[32m"java:"[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlocal Java naming context[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Reject dangerous remote schemes: `[0m[32m"ldap:"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"ldaps:"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"rmi:"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"dns:"[0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"iiop:"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"corba:"[0m[39m`, etc.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Add validation in the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent event, String key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method after the [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Existing Applications Using JNDI Lookups**[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Applications using `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` in configuration will stop working[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Clear documentation that JNDI must be explicitly enabled[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Detection**: Applications will log warnings when JNDI lookups are attempted but[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabled[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Test Failures**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: `JndiLookupTest.java` might fail if ENABLE_JNDI defaults to false[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The test already checks `[0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m53[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m55[0m[39m, so it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill skip gracefully[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Alternative**: Tests can programmatically enable JNDI via [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.setEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in setup[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remote LDAP/RMI Lookups**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Legitimate remote JNDI lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any exist[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be blocked[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The URL validation only allows `java:` scheme, which is the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocumented use case[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Justification**: Remote JNDI lookups are inherently dangerous and should not be[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformed from logging[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in the Codebase[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows established patterns in Log4j:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **System Property Pattern**: Similar to `LOG4J_DEFAULT_STATUS_LEVEL` [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mConstants.java line [0m[1;36m36[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **PropertiesUtil Usage**: Similar to `[0m[1;35mBaseConfiguration.getDefaultStatus[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m157[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Feature Flags**: Similar to how other features are controlled through system [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperties[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Validation**: Similar pattern to SecurityManager checks in other [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparts of the codebase[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with Alternative Approaches[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove JndiLookup Entirely**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pros**: Complete elimination of attack surface[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cons**: Breaking change for legitimate users, no migration path[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Verdict**: Too disruptive[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Disable Message Lookup**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pros**: Prevents all message-based attacks[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cons**: Breaks legitimate use of $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39msys:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m, $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39menv:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m, etc.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Verdict**: Too broad, affects safe features[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Escape-Only Fix**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pros**: Minimal changes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cons**: Requires all applications to sanitize input, error-prone[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Verdict**: Not sufficient, puts burden on users[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Allowlist-Based JNDI**[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pros**: Flexible for different use cases[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cons**: Complex configuration, still allows JNDI[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Verdict**: More complex than needed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Our Approach: Disable + Validate + Conditional**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pros**: Secure by default, backward compatible via flag, defense in depth[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cons**: Requires explicit enablement for JNDI users[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Verdict**: Best balance of security and compatibility[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
